>>> item >>> {'indexed': {'date-parts': [[2018, 5, 8]], 'date-time': '2018-05-08T09:02:26Z', 'timestamp': 1525770146830}, 'reference-count': 0, 'publisher': 'Walter de Gruyter GmbH', 'issue': '1', 'license': [{'URL': 'http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-nd/4.0', 'start': {'date-parts': [[2004, 12, 1]], 'date-time': '2004-12-01T00:00:00Z', 'timestamp': 1101859200000}, 'delay-in-days': 0, 'content-version': 'unspecified'}], 'content-domain': {'domain': [], 'crossmark-restriction': False}, 'published-print': {'date-parts': [[2004, 12, 1]]}, 'abstract': '<jats:title>Summary</jats:title><jats:p>We propose a method for visualizing a set of related metabolic pathways across organisms using 2 1/2 dimensional graph visualization. Interdependent, twodimensional layouts of each pathway are stacked on top of each other so that biologists get a full picture of subtle and significant differences among the pathways. The (dis)similarities between pathways are expressed by the Hamming distances of the underlying graphs which are used to compute a stacking order for the pathways. Layouts are determined by a global layout of the union of all pathway graphs using a variant of the proven Sugiyama approach for layered graph drawing. Our variant layout approach allows edges to cross if they appear in different graphs.</jats:p>', 'DOI': '10.1515/jib-2004-2', 'type': 'journal-article', 'created': {'date-parts': [[2017, 12, 7]], 'date-time': '2017-12-07T15:35:32Z', 'timestamp': 1512660932000}, 'source': 'Crossref', 'is-referenced-by-count': 0, 'title': ['Visual Understanding of Metabolic Pathways Across Organisms Using Layout in Two and a Half Dimensions'], 'prefix': '10.1515', 'volume': '1', 'author': [{'given': 'Ulrik', 'family': 'Brandes', 'sequence': 'first', 'affiliation': []}, {'given': 'Tim', 'family': 'Dwyer', 'sequence': 'additional', 'affiliation': []}, {'given': 'Falk', 'family': 'Schreiber', 'sequence': 'additional', 'affiliation': []}], 'member': '374', 'container-title': ['Journal of Integrative Bioinformatics'], 'link': [{'URL': 'http://www.degruyter.com/view/j/jib.2004.1.issue-1/biecoll-jib-2004-2/biecoll-jib-2004-2.xml', 'content-type': 'text/html', 'content-version': 'vor', 'intended-application': 'text-mining'}, {'URL': 'http://www.degruyter.com/view/j/jib.2004.1.issue-1/biecoll-jib-2004-2/biecoll-jib-2004-2.pdf', 'content-type': 'unspecified', 'content-version': 'vor', 'intended-application': 'similarity-checking'}], 'deposited': {'date-parts': [[2017, 12, 7]], 'date-time': '2017-12-07T22:17:11Z', 'timestamp': 1512685031000}, 'score': 107.795975, 'issued': {'date-parts': [[2004, 12, 1]]}, 'references-count': 0, 'journal-issue': {'issue': '1'}, 'URL': 'http://dx.doi.org/10.1515/jib-2004-2', 'ISSN': ['1613-4516'], 'issn-type': [{'value': '1613-4516', 'type': 'electronic'}]}
